 9
 navazuddin siddiki ko shivasena ne unke gaanv main nahin karne di 'ramlila' Film actor Nawazuddin Siddiqui was not allowed by the Shiv Sena to perform Ramlila in his village
 navazuddin mujffarnagar ke budhaanaa gaanv ke rahane vaale hai
 The people of the Ramlila committee of his village wanted Nawazuddin Siddiqui to play the role of Marich in Ramlila
 navazuddin ne iske liye kaaphi reharsal kii thi
 He arrived there yesterday to join Ramlila
 vahaan green room main taiyaar ho rahe the tabhi shivasena ke logon ne vahaan pahunchakar unka virodh kiya, jiske baad nawaz chupchaap vahaan se ghar waapas chale gaye

 Detailed warnings have been sent to 22 airports in four cities and officials confirm that arrangements are being made to ensure high security measures at these places

 Good news: now the problem of getting approval from the employer to remove PF will end pief nikaalane ke liye karmchaariyon ko ab amploir se manjuuri nahin leni hogi
 Now the employees will not have to get any kind of certified documents from their former employer company under the new rules of EPFO
 kul milakar ab aapako pief kaa paisa nikalwane ke liye puraani company ke chakkar nahin lagane padenge

 upra : chachaa shivpal yadav ke saamne nahin chali akhilesh kii, kaumi ekta dal kaa sapa main vilay Despite opposition from Uttar Pradesh Chief Minister Akhilesh Yadav, the Qaumi Ekta Dal (kaued) was finally merged with the Samajwadi Party (SP)
 isse pehle akhilesh ke hath ke aage vilay ko radd kar diya gaya tha
 SP state president Shivpal Yadav said that Mulayam Singh decided to merge
 iske liye akhilesh se bhi salaah lee gai
 With all unhone kaha ki netaji (mulaayam singh yadav) ne kah diya to samajho vilay ho gaya

 railway kaa festival ofer : yatriyon ko sirf 1 paise main milegaa 10 lakh kaa beemaa cover

 is ofer kaa laabh 7 se lekar 31 oktober tak internet se tikat book karne vaale yatriyon ko milegaa

 kamitment kii nai misaal bane mohammad shami, beti ko isiu main chhod bharat ko jitayaa
 
 
 In the second match of the 3 Test match series played in Kolkata, Team India defeated New Zealand to take the number one position in the ICC rankings, but in this team India fast bowlers played an important role
 khaastaur se tej gendbaaj mohammad shami kaa, jinhone donon pariyon main 3-3 wicket chatkaakar team kii jeet pakki kar di
 Shami's performance became special for another reason
 unhone is match main kamitment kii anuthi misaal pesh kii or beti ke gambhir rup se biimaar hone ke baavjood khel ke prati puri tarah se samarpit rahe

 yah baat 68 varshiya rajaneta kaa ilaaj kar rahe doctoron ne kahi

 9
 Shiv Sena did not allow Nawazuddin Siddiqui to do Ramlila in his village film abhinayta navazuddin siddiki ko shivasena ne unke gaanv main ramlila nahin karne di
 Nawazuddin hails from Budhana village of Muzaffarnagar
 unke gaanv kii ramlila cameti ke log chaahate the ki navazuddin siddiki ramlila main marich kaa role karen
 Nawazuddin did a lot of rehearsals for this
 vah kal ramlila main shaamil hone ke liye vahaan pahunche
 While the people were getting ready in the green room, Shiv Sena people reached there and opposed them, after which Nawaz quietly went back home from there
